    - Sample synth benchmark:
      - edge avg ~1995.8ms
      - vieneu avg ~2168.6ms
  - Tradeoff:
    - First-audio may be slightly later than chunk-stream start, but speech continuity is significantly more natural and avoids word-by-word choppiness.

- Enhancement round 130 completed (VieNeu realtime research + player bug fix):
  - User request:
    - Keep VieNeu voice quality and enable true realtime smooth speech (no word-by-word pauses).
  - Internet research summary:
    - Reviewed VieNeu-TTS repo docs and streaming demo implementation.
    - Key finding: VieNeu realtime demo streams WAV header then PCM chunks and plays with AudioContext scheduling, not per-chunk <audio> elements.
  - Root cause in project:
    - Kiosk player treated WAV chunks as separate audio files (new Audio/Blob per chunk), introducing audible gaps and fragmented speech.
  - Fix applied:
    - `apps/kiosk-ui/public/stitch_robot_3d_control_center.html`
      - Added `playVieneuWavStream()` using AudioContext + PCM scheduling for continuous playback.
      - Added WAV sample-rate parsing and repeated-header stripping logic for backend compatibility.
      - Updated `playBotSpeech()` engine routing:
        - if VieNeu requested/selected -> use VieNeu realtime stream path.
        - else keep fast edge blob fallback path.
      - Kept abort handling and UI face-state transitions consistent.
  - Validation:
    - `npm run build:ui` passed.
  - Impact:
    - VieNeu realtime now follows the same playback model as upstream demo behavior, removing chunk boundary pauses that sounded like one-word speech.

- Enhancement round 131 completed (auto-greeting immediate + voice prewarm):
  - User issue:
    - Presence detection showed greeting text but often failed to speak immediately, status showed `Khong tao duoc loi chao tu dong.`
  - Root causes addressed:
    - Auto-greeting path hard-failed when `startConversationSession('camera')` failed once.
    - First audio path could be blocked/suspended (autoplay/audio context warm-up not ready).
    - Interrupt logic did not cancel browser `speechSynthesis`, causing stale speech overlap risk.
  - Fixes applied:
    - `apps/kiosk-ui/public/stitch_robot_3d_control_center.html`
      - Added `AUTO_GREETING_FALLBACK_TEXT` so greeting still speaks even if session bootstrap fails.
      - Added runtime prewarm (`prewarmVoiceRuntime`) called on kiosk init to warm AI URL probe and audio context unlock hooks.
      - Added autoplay detection (`isAutoplayBlockedError`) and browser TTS fallback helper (`speakWithBrowserFallback`).
      - Updated `playVieneuWavStream` to resume suspended `AudioContext` before scheduling PCM chunks.
      - Updated `playBotSpeech` fallback behavior: if stream/blob playback is blocked, fallback to browser speech instead of silent failure.
      - Updated `interruptBotSpeech` to also cancel `window.speechSynthesis`.
      - Refactored `runAutoGreeting` to be graceful:
        - try backend session greeting first,
        - fallback to default greeting if backend not ready,
        - keep status in ready/listening state instead of hard error.
  - Validation:
    - `npm --prefix apps/kiosk-ui run build` passed.
  - Expected impact:
    - On presence enter, robot should greet immediately more consistently.
    - Auto-greeting no longer gets stuck in hard-fail status when backend startup is slow.
    - Better first-audio reliability on kiosk browsers with autoplay restrictions.

- Debug round 132 completed (auto-greeting root cause fix, removed browser voice fallback):
  - Symptom:
    - Presence detected but greeting often failed early with status `Khong tao duoc loi chao tu dong.`
    - Browser fallback voice was used in some failures and sounded unnatural for Vietnamese.
  - Evidence collected:
    - Runtime `/health` showed AI backend healthy with `tts_engine=vieneu` and `vieneu_installed=true`.
    - `/sessions/start` can fail if core backend is unavailable because greeting build path still fetched menu.
    - Existing kiosk logic set cooldown timestamp before greeting success, so a first failed attempt delayed immediate retry.
  - Root cause:
    1) Backend `start_session()` indirectly depended on `core_client.list_menu()` via `_build_response()`, which is unnecessary for an empty-cart greeting and causes startup-time greeting failure.
    2) UI auto-greeting cooldown and retry behavior were not robust for backend cold-start races.
    3) Browser `speechSynthesis` fallback masked root cause and produced poor Vietnamese voice quality.
  - Fixes applied:
    - `services/ai-backend/app/services/conversation_engine.py`
      - `start_session()` now calls `_build_response(..., menu=[])`.
      - `_build_response()` now fetches menu only when `menu is None` (not for explicit empty list).
    - `services/ai-backend/tests/test_ai_backend.py`
      - Added `test_start_session_does_not_require_core_menu` to prevent regression.
    - `apps/kiosk-ui/public/stitch_robot_3d_control_center.html`
      - Removed browser speech fallback flow (no `speechSynthesis` fallback playback).
      - Added auto-greeting retry scheduler with bounded retries/backoff.
      - Moved cooldown update to success path only (`lastAutoGreetingAt` set after successful spoken greeting).
      - Kept audio/runtime prewarm and added VieNeu stream warmup call.
      - On autoplay-blocked errors, status now shows clear unblock instruction instead of fallback voice.
  - Validation:
    - `pytest services/ai-backend/tests/test_ai_backend.py -q` passed (34 passed).
    - `npm --prefix apps/kiosk-ui run build` passed.
  - Remaining risks:
    - If browser autoplay policy blocks audio output before any user interaction, speech still cannot start; UI now reports explicit unblock message instead of switching to low-quality fallback voice.

- Enhance round 133 completed (triage and hardening for noisy AI logs + VieNeu cold-start latency):
  - User pain:
    - Need clear actionable logs for real errors.

    - First TTS request can be very slow due VieNeu model load on-demand.
  - Root causes:
    1) VieNeu model was initialized lazily on first synth request, so `Loading weights ...` happened during customer interaction.

    3) Backend lacked structured TTS stage logs (first chunk / total latency / bytes), making root-cause diagnosis slow.

      - Added `preload_tts()` + `_preload_vieneu_sync()` to pre-initialize VieNeu at startup.
      - Added `get_vieneu_diagnostics()` for explicit runtime visibility.
      - Added structured init logs (`vieneu_init_ok`, `vieneu_init_failed`, `vieneu_ready`).
      - Added structured TTS latency logs:
        - stream: `tts_stream_ms`, `tts_first_chunk_ms`, `chunks`, `bytes`.

    - `services/ai-backend/app/main.py`
      - Startup now schedules both STT preload and TTS preload tasks.
      - Added `GET /speech/vieneu/diag` endpoint to inspect VieNeu runtime status.
      - Added endpoint-level TTS logs for `/speech/synthesize` and `/speech/synthesize/stream` including total latency + error path logs.
    - Dev scripts logging cleanup:
      - `scripts/dev-ai.ps1`, `scripts/dev-ai-lite.ps1`, `scripts/dev-core.ps1` now run uvicorn directly (removed `2>&1 | ForEach-Object { Write-Host $_ }`) to avoid PowerShell `RemoteException` log noise.

- Debug round 138 completed (VieNeu stream stutter root-cause + fixes):
  - Symptom:
    - VieNeu speech still sounded cut/choppy even when chat text was correct.
  - Evidence:
    - Stream probe on `/speech/synthesize/stream` showed repeated `RIFF` per chunk with chunk cadence around 1.3-1.7s for ~0.5s audio payload.
    - Direct SDK probe showed CPU `infer_stream` throughput below realtime; high playback rate amplified underruns.
  - Root causes:
    1) Backend stream path wrapped numpy chunks into full WAV every chunk (repeated header), not matching VieNeu realtime pattern.
    2) No active preempt signal for stale VieNeu stream jobs, so newer requests could wait behind old stream work.
    3) Kiosk default stream playback rate (`1.08`) was too aggressive for current CPU throughput.
  - Fixes applied:
    - `services/ai-backend/app/services/speech_service.py`
      - Emit WAV header once + PCM16 chunk payload for ndarray stream chunks.
      - Add VieNeu stream preempt/cancel guard (new stream cancels previous active stream worker).
      - Add stream diagnostics (`audio_sec`, `realtime_factor`) and expose factor in `/speech/vieneu/diag`.
      - Add runtime stream tuning apply (`frames_per_chunk`, `lookforward`, `lookback`, `overlap`).
    - `services/ai-backend/app/config.py`
      - Added env settings:
        - `TTS_VIENEU_STREAM_FRAMES_PER_CHUNK`
        - `TTS_VIENEU_STREAM_LOOKFORWARD`
        - `TTS_VIENEU_STREAM_LOOKBACK`
        - `TTS_VIENEU_STREAM_OVERLAP_FRAMES`
    - `services/ai-backend/app/models.py`
      - Extended `TTSConfigRequest` with stream tuning fields + legacy aliases.
    - `services/ai-backend/app/main.py`
      - `/health` and `/config/tts` now include VieNeu stream tuning fields.
      - `/speech/synthesize/stream` returns `audio/wav` when engine is explicitly VieNeu.
    - `apps/kiosk-ui/public/stitch_robot_3d_control_center.html`
      - Set default `TTS_STREAM_PLAYBACK_RATE` to `1.0` (clamp `0.75-1.1`).
      - Add small prebuffer (2 chunks) before playback to reduce immediate underrun artifacts.
    - `apps/kiosk-ui/src/AdminPage.tsx`
      - Added admin env controls for VieNeu stream tuning.
      - Updated preset defaults with safer playback rate `1.0`.
  - Validation:
    - `pytest services/ai-backend/tests/test_speech_service.py -q` -> 22 passed.
    - `pytest services/ai-backend/tests/test_ai_backend.py -q` -> 34 passed.
    - `npm --prefix apps/kiosk-ui run build` -> passed.
  - Remaining risk:
    - CPU-only VieNeu stream can still run below realtime on long sentences; use `realtime_factor` logs to tune or move to faster backend mode.

- Enhance round 139 completed (VieNeu multi-mode support + anti-stutter runtime strategy):
  - User pain:
    - VieNeu still stuttered despite prior stream-format fixes; user expected realtime capability from official docs.
  - Additional findings:
    - Current stack always initialized VieNeu factory without mode/device controls, effectively locking runtime to default standard/cpu behavior.
    - Official VieNeu supports multiple inference modes (`standard`, `fast/gpu`, `xpu`, `remote`) and realtime claims are mainly aligned with fast/GPU paths.
    - On current CPU standard mode, measured stream throughput remained below realtime, which can cause audible underrun/stutter during live stream playback.
  - Fixes applied:
    - `services/ai-backend/app/config.py`
      - Added VieNeu runtime fields:
        - `TTS_VIENEU_MODE`
        - `TTS_VIENEU_BACKBONE_DEVICE`
        - `TTS_VIENEU_CODEC_REPO`
        - `TTS_VIENEU_CODEC_DEVICE`
        - `TTS_VIENEU_REMOTE_API_BASE`
    - `services/ai-backend/app/models.py`
      - Extended `TTSConfigRequest` with matching fields + legacy aliases.
    - `services/ai-backend/app/main.py`
      - `/health` now exposes VieNeu mode/device fields and `vieneu_stream_realtime_factor`.
      - `/config/tts` now updates/returns VieNeu mode/device settings and resets runtime when changed.
    - `services/ai-backend/app/services/speech_service.py`
      - VieNeu init now respects configured mode/device/remote settings:
        - `Vieneu(mode=<configured_mode>, **kwargs)`
      - Added mode-aware init attempts and logging (`vieneu_init_ok/failed` include mode).
      - Diagnostics now include mode/device/remote config for faster triage.
    - `apps/kiosk-ui/src/AdminPage.tsx`
      - Added admin env controls for VieNeu mode/device/remote fields.
      - Updated realtime profiles:
        - CPU profile -> `standard/cpu`
        - GPU profiles -> `fast/cuda`
      - `/config/tts` payload now sends the new mode/device fields.
    - `apps/kiosk-ui/public/stitch_robot_3d_control_center.html`
      - Added `isVieneuRealtimeCapable()` gate:
        - stream playback only when mode is `fast/xpu` or backend reports high realtime factor.
      - If not realtime-capable, keep VieNeu voice but switch to full synth playback path (smooth speech, no word-by-word jitter).
      - Stream prewarm now only runs for `fast/xpu` mode.
  - Validation:
    - `python -m compileall ...` passed for updated backend files.
    - `pytest services/ai-backend/tests/test_speech_service.py -q` -> 22 passed.
    - `pytest services/ai-backend/tests/test_ai_backend.py -q` -> 34 passed.
    - `npm --prefix apps/kiosk-ui run build` -> passed.
  - Remaining note:
    - To get true low-latency realtime streaming, runtime should use VieNeu fast-capable backend (`TTS_VIENEU_MODE=fast`) with compatible GPU stack.

- Enhance round 143 completed (two-tier routing + faster perceived TTS response):
  - User pain:
    - Voice flow still felt slow versus Grok-style interaction.

      - cached filler prompts and delayed filler injection while waiting (can be interrupted when real answer starts).

      - stream path uses bridge for hard query and avoids extra blocking `compose_reply` call,
      - fast recommendation path skips bridge for simple query.
  - Tradeoffs:
    - Hard-query detection is heuristic/rule-based and may need threshold tuning from real logs.
    - Filler audio improves perceived speed but can briefly play before the final answer starts in slower turns.
  - Remaining tech debt:
    - Add admin-exposed router thresholds for live tuning (keyword/length/confidence) without code changes.

- Enhance round 144 completed (additional latency cut: early speak from stream + stricter bridge escalation):
  - User request:
    - Continue optimizing because perceived speed was still behind Grok-like instant response.
  - Backend optimization (`services/ai-backend/app/services/conversation_engine.py`):
    - Tightened bridge escalation thresholds to keep more turns on fast local path:
      - `BRIDGE_LONG_QUERY_WORDS_THRESHOLD: 20` (was 16)
      - `BRIDGE_LONG_QUERY_CHARS_THRESHOLD: 120` (was 90)
      - Removed question-mark-only escalation condition.
    - Result: fewer unnecessary bridge calls for medium short conversational turns.
  - Frontend optimization (`apps/kiosk-ui/public/stitch_robot_3d_control_center.html`):
    - Added progressive speech strategy for stream text:
      - New helpers: `extractEarlySpeakableText(...)`, `removeSpokenPrefixText(...)`.
      - Bot can start speaking a stable lead segment (ending at punctuation) before full final text arrives.
      - On final text, only speaks the remaining tail to avoid repeating the full sentence.
    - Improved UX masking while waiting:
      - filler prompt timer retained and auto-canceled when early speech starts.
      - if filler is already playing, it is interrupted cleanly before real answer speech.
    - Added minimum lead threshold `STREAM_EARLY_SPEECH_MIN_CHARS=42` to avoid reading too-short fragments.
  - Validation:
    - `pytest services/ai-backend/tests/test_ai_backend.py -q` -> 38 passed.
    - `pytest services/ai-backend/tests/test_speech_service.py -q` -> 22 passed.
    - `npm --prefix apps/kiosk-ui run build` -> passed.
  - Expected impact:
    - Lower delay from first visible text to first meaningful speech.
    - Less dependence on bridge latency for everyday short queries.
  - Remaining tuning ideas:
    - Expose early-speech threshold and bridge escalation thresholds in Admin for live tuning.
    - Add shared persistent AudioContext for WS TTS path to cut per-call setup overhead further.

- Debug round 113 completed (partial STT decode error in streaming WebM):
  - Symptom:
    - Partial STT spammed `av.error.InvalidDataError` while processing `speech.webm`.
  - Root cause:
    - Partial audio snapshots can be incomplete WebM chunks; decoder may fail transiently before enough bytes arrive.
  - Fix applied:
    - In `services/ai-backend/app/services/speech_service.py`, `_transcribe_partial_sync` now catches decode-only partial errors and returns empty transcript.
    - Added `_is_partial_decode_error` helper to classify known PyAV/FFmpeg decode failures.
    - Final/full transcription path is unchanged.
  - Verification:
    - `python -m py_compile services/ai-backend/app/services/speech_service.py` passed.
  - Remaining risk:
    - Truly malformed stream packets still result in no partial text until final decode attempt.

- Debug round 145 completed (partial STT PyAV tuple-index crash in streaming):
  - Symptom:
    - Partial STT sometimes crashed with `IndexError: tuple index out of range` from `av.container.streams.StreamContainer.get` while decoding streaming snapshots.
  - Root cause:
    - Existing partial decode guard handled known FFmpeg/PyAV invalid-data EOF signatures, but did not classify this PyAV tuple-index variant seen on incomplete WebM partial chunks.
  - Fix applied:
    - `services/ai-backend/app/services/speech_service.py`
      - Extended `_is_partial_decode_error` to detect this variant via:
        - message marker `tuple index out of range`
        - traceback markers under decode stack (`faster_whisper/audio.py`, `av/container/input.py`, `av/container/streams.py`) for `IndexError`.
    - `services/ai-backend/tests/test_speech_service.py`
      - Added regression tests for decode-like `IndexError` classification and non-decode `IndexError` passthrough.
  - Verification:
    - `python -m py_compile services/ai-backend/app/services/speech_service.py services/ai-backend/tests/test_speech_service.py` passed.
    - Full pytest run in current shell failed at collection due missing local dependency `edge_tts`.
  - Remaining risk:
    - If PyAV introduces another novel decode signature, markers may need future extension; final/full STT flow remains unchanged.

- Enhance round 146 completed (bridge sentence-streaming + keepalive + SSE stream endpoint):
  - User goal:
    - Reduce first-audio latency by speaking sentence-by-sentence while bridge is still generating.
    - Eliminate bridge cold-start delay from idle periods.
  - Improvements applied:
    - `services/ai-backend/app/services/provider_client.py`
      - Upgraded `compose_reply_stream(...)` to accumulate token deltas and emit sentence-complete chunks on punctuation (`. ! ? ŃĆé ’╝ü ’╝¤ \n`) instead of tiny token fragments.
      - Added stream helpers `append_stream_content(...)` and `split_completed_sentences(...)`.
      - Added `ping(...)` method with `/ping` -> `/health` fallback for keepalive probes.
    - `services/ai-backend/app/config.py`
      - Added bridge keepalive settings:
        - `BRIDGE_KEEPALIVE_ENABLED` (default true)
        - `BRIDGE_KEEPALIVE_INTERVAL_SECONDS` (default 90)
        - `BRIDGE_KEEPALIVE_TIMEOUT_SECONDS` (default 5)
    - `services/ai-backend/app/main.py`
      - Added startup background keepalive task `_bridge_keepalive_loop()` and clean cancellation on shutdown.
      - `/health` now exposes keepalive runtime settings.
      - Added SSE endpoint `GET /chat/stream?session_id=...&text=...` returning `data: {"sentence": "..."}` chunks and `[DONE]` sentinel.
    - `scripts/bridge-server.mjs`
      - Added `GET /ping` lightweight 200 OK endpoint for low-cost keepalive.
    - `services/ai-backend/app/services/conversation_engine.py`
      - Added static keyword fast-cache path for short common utterances (greeting/menu/confirm) to return immediate local response without bridge roundtrip where applicable.
  - Validation:
    - `pytest services/ai-backend/tests/test_ai_backend.py -q -k "not trio"` -> 25 passed, 16 deselected.
    - `python -m py_compile` for updated backend modules -> passed.
    - Note: full anyio matrix still requires local `trio` package in this shell.
  - Tradeoffs / risks:
    - Sentence-gated stream may defer output for very long punctuation-less replies; final tail still flushes at end.
    - Static keyword cache is limited to short queries to avoid over-matching.
  - Frontend streaming TTS update:
    - `apps/kiosk-ui/public/stitch_robot_3d_control_center.html` now queues and plays incremental sentence segments during text stream (`earlySpeechQueuePromise`) instead of speaking only one early prefix then waiting for final tail.
    - Result: speech can continue sentence-by-sentence while bridge still generating next content.

- Enhance round 147 completed (bridge routing for non-ordering speech + anti-false-recommendation):
  - User pain point:
    - Non-ordering utterances (`tao ten la danh`, profanity, random chitchat) were incorrectly mapped to `recommendation` and returned static local menu suggestions.
    - Bridge stream was skipped for these turns, causing bot to feel "khong hieu" and repetitive.
  - Root causes:
    - Fallback recommendation path accepted any positive rank score, even weak token overlap.
    - `_rank_items` accepted short noise tokens, increasing accidental score.
    - `_should_use_bridge` defaulted to local template for most `fallback` and contextual `greeting` turns.
  - Fix applied:
    - Tightened recommendation gating:
      - Require top rank score >= `_MIN_RANK_SCORE_FOR_RECOMMENDATION` in both recommend-keyword branch and generic rank fallback.
      - Generic rank fallback now only applies when `has_ordering_hint` is true.
    - Reduced noisy token scoring in `_rank_items` by skipping tokens with length <= 2.
    - Improved bridge routing:
      - `fallback` now routes to bridge for profanity/chitchat/meaningful short context (>=2 tokens), local only for tiny noise.
      - `greeting` now routes simple greetings locally, but contextual greeting/chitchat to bridge.
    - Added helpers:
      - `_contains_profanity_text`
      - `_is_simple_greeting_text`
    - Refined `_is_chitchat` short-text heuristic from <=3 chars to <=2 chars.
  - Tests added:
    - `test_handle_turn_stream_routes_self_intro_to_greeting_bridge_scene`
    - `test_handle_turn_stream_routes_profanity_to_bridge_fallback_scene`
    - `test_non_ordering_chat_does_not_fall_into_recommendation_scene`
  - Validation:
    - `pytest services/ai-backend/tests/test_ai_backend.py -q -k "not trio"` -> 28 passed, 19 deselected.
    - `python -m py_compile services/ai-backend/app/services/conversation_engine.py services/ai-backend/tests/test_ai_backend.py` passed.
  - Tradeoff:
    - Bridge traffic increases on contextual fallback/greeting turns; improves conversational correctness but may add small inference cost.

- Debug round 375 completed (VieNeu CPU buzzing/noisy output + wrong preset/runtime defaults):
  - Symptom:
    - User still heard `∙ ∙` noise and unstable voice output after upgrade; logs repeatedly showed `VieNeu preset voice 'Doan' not found`.

    - Direct probes on current machine showed Turbo GGUF + current admin/backend defaults produced very long/noisy waveform (~31.8s for short test sentence).

    - CPU default/preset selected an unstable Turbo path for this integration/runtime profile.

    - Float waveform conversion used hard clipping; this could increase harsh distortion when peaks exceeded 1.0.

      - Added preset voice alias resolver (`_resolve_vieneu_voice_alias`) so shorthand like `Doan` can map to real preset IDs.
      - Improved float-to-PCM conversion with peak normalization before int16 quantization to reduce clipping artifacts.
    - `apps/kiosk-ui/src/AdminPage.tsx`
      - Changed env template and CPU realtime preset default model to `0.3B-q4`.
      - Set CPU realtime preset codec repo to auto (`''`) instead of forcing legacy ONNX codec string.

- Debug round 377 completed (VieNeu v2 Turbo GGUF overflow + wrong mode routing):
  - Symptom:
    - Repeated `502` on `/speech/synthesize` and stream path with error `Requested tokens (...) exceed context window of 2048`.

      - Added `_normalize_vieneu_mode(...)` with support for `turbo` / `turbo_gpu`.

      - Added turbo init kwargs path (`backbone_repo` + `device`).
      - For turbo model, ignores custom `codec_repo` and uses SDK defaults.
      - Turbo voice selection now passes preset via `ref_codes` (instead of only `voice`).
    - `services/ai-backend/app/config.py`
      - Default `TTS_VIENEU_MODE` switched from `standard` to `turbo`.
    - `services/ai-backend/app/main.py`
      - Runtime config API now accepts `turbo` and `turbo_gpu`.
    - `apps/kiosk-ui/src/AdminPage.tsx`
      - Admin defaults/profile updated to `turbo` for CPU realtime v2 Turbo GGUF.

      - Warmup gate now allows `turbo` / `turbo_gpu`.
  - Validation:
    - `python -m compileall services/ai-backend/app/config.py services/ai-backend/app/main.py services/ai-backend/app/services/speech_service.py` passed.

- Debug round 379 completed (Turbo preset voice always sounded like one voice):
  - Symptom:
    - User selected different VieNeu preset voices but output still sounded like the same voice.
  - Evidence:
    - Hugging Face model card for `pnnbao-ump/VieNeu-TTS-v2-Turbo-GGUF` uses `tts.infer(..., voice=voice_data)` for preset voice.

    - Admin apply/test logic could enter clone mode (`ref_audio` + `ref_text`) and clear `vieneu_voice_id`, forcing default voice.
    - Remote/local `voices.json` for this model currently reports 4 preset voices (not 6).

    - `services/ai-backend/app/services/speech_service.py`
      - For turbo runtime, now sets both `voice` and `ref_codes` so sync and stream endpoints both receive preset voice correctly.
      - Added explicit log `vieneu_voice_selected id=... turbo=...` for debugging.
    - `apps/kiosk-ui/src/AdminPage.tsx`
      - In Turbo mode, clone fields are ignored for apply/test payload (no auto-clearing into default voice path).
      - Preset validation still enforced against loaded runtime voice list.
  - Validation:
    - `python -m compileall ...` passed.
    - `npm --prefix apps/kiosk-ui run build` passed.
    - Local inspection confirmed turbo infer kwargs now include both `voice` and `ref_codes`, and embeddings differ by selected voice IDs.
- Debug round 380 completed (Vietnamese reply spacing artifacts like `kh¶ngph ?c`, `²cho`):
  - Symptom:
    - Assistant text occasionally had glued/split Vietnamese words in one sentence.
  - Root cause:
    - Existing safe-reply guard mainly detected severe corruption; it did not actively repair common spacing artifacts.
  - Fixes applied:
    - `services/ai-backend/app/services/conversation_engine.py`
      - Added `_repair_vietnamese_spacing_text(...)` before safety checks.
      - Added targeted regex rules to:
        - insert missing spaces after commonly glued Vietnamese function words,
        - merge broken consonant clusters split by accidental spaces.
    - `services/ai-backend/tests/test_ai_backend.py`
      - Added regression test using real broken sentence pattern from user (`kh¶ngph ?c`, `g?i ²cho`).
  - Validation:
    - `pytest -q services/ai-backend/tests/test_ai_backend.py -k "ensure_frontend_safe_reply"` -> 3 passed.
- Debug round 381 completed (mic noise filter slider had little practical effect on backend STT):
  - Symptom:
    - User changed mic noise filter strength in admin, but recognition quality/noise rejection barely changed.
  - Root cause:
    - Kiosk backend STT path relied mostly on `getUserMedia` constraints only.
    - Browser-level `noiseSuppression/echoCancellation` are device/browser dependent and can feel ineffective.
  - Fixes applied:
    - `apps/kiosk-ui/public/stitch_robot_3d_control_center.html`
      - Added explicit WebAudio preprocessing chain for backend STT stream:
        - high-pass filter (remove low hum),
        - low-pass filter (reduce hiss),
        - dynamics compressor (stabilize speech level).
      - Strength slider now maps to filter/compressor aggressiveness.
      - Added processing teardown/cleanup and fallback-to-raw stream if processing fails.
      - Restart path keeps applying new strength by rebuilding backend mic stream.
  - Validation:
    - `npm --prefix apps/kiosk-ui run build` passed.

- Enhance round 382 completed (stabilize VN intent parsing + STT alias robustness in conversation engine):
  - User pain point:
    - Chat flow unstable for STT-misheard commands like `gui di/gui y di`, and some order utterances failed to add items (e.g. `capuchino`).
    - Recommendation requests could fall through to weak fallback responses instead of clear menu suggestions.
  - Root causes:
    - `normalize_text(...)` dropped Vietnamese `d-with-stroke`, degrading intent words (`dat`, `di`, `goi y`).
    - Early `handle_turn(...)` intent checks ran before STT alias correction.
    - Recommendation branch required high rank threshold and skipped useful suggestions for short generic queries.
  - Fixes applied:
    - `services/ai-backend/app/services/conversation_engine.py`
      - Preserve Vietnamese `d-with-stroke` as `d` during normalization.
      - Added aliases: `gui di`, `gui y di`, `gui y`, `gui i`, `goi i`, and `capuchino/capuccino/...` -> `cappuccino`.
      - Apply STT alias correction at start of `handle_turn(...)` so early intent routing uses corrected text.
      - Recommendation-intent path now always returns actionable suggestions even when rank score is weak.
    - `services/ai-backend/tests/test_ai_backend.py`
      - Added regressions for normalize (`Dat di`), `gui di` recommendation route, and `capuchino` -> `Cappuccino` add flow.
  - Validation:
    - Ran targeted pytest nodes on asyncio backend: 5 passed.
  - Tradeoff:
    - Alias mapping remains rule-based; uncommon STT mistakes may still require future alias expansion.

- Enhance round 383 completed (harden add/remove/order flow against latest menu API state):
  - User pain point:
    - Wanted add/remove mechanism to strictly follow products currently available in API menu.
  - Risks found:
    - Checkout could still submit stale cart item IDs if menu changed after adding items.
    - Remove-intent fallback could delete last cart item even when user asked to remove a specific unknown item.
  - Fixes applied:
    - `services/ai-backend/app/services/conversation_engine.py`
      - Added cart pruning before confirmation/checkout: remove cart items no longer present in API menu or marked unavailable.
      - If cart became empty after prune, return recommendation prompt (no order submission).
      - If cart still has items after prune, require reconfirmation with clear explanation.
      - Added safer remove behavior: fallback remove-last-item now only triggers for generic remove commands; specific unknown remove no longer drops unrelated cart item.
      - Added explicit feedback when remove target is not found in current cart.
    - `services/ai-backend/tests/test_ai_backend.py`
      - Added regression: unknown remove request does not remove last cart item.
      - Added regression: checkout prunes items removed from latest API menu and blocks order creation.
  - Validation:
    - Targeted pytest on asyncio backend: 4 passed.
    - `python -m py_compile` for changed backend/test files passed.
  - Tradeoff:
    - Cart now enforces strict API consistency at checkout time; if menu changes frequently, users may be asked to reconfirm more often.

- Enhance round 384 completed (quantity add/remove accuracy hardening):
  - User ask:
    - Re-check whether quantity increment/decrement flow is truly precise and stable.
  - Findings:
    - Generic decrement phrases like `bot 1 ly` and `bot hai` were not routed to remove flow because `REMOVE_KEYWORDS` missed `bot`.
    - Generic remove fallback now supports quantity parsing but needed keyword alignment to activate reliably.
  - Fixes applied:
    - `services/ai-backend/app/services/conversation_engine.py`
      - Added `bot` and `giam` to `REMOVE_KEYWORDS`.
      - Improved generic remove safety/precision:
        - keep fallback remove-last only for generic remove utterances,
        - parse quantity from generic remove phrases,
        - decrement quantity instead of deleting full line by default.
      - Expanded generic remove parser to accept number tokens/number words/unit words (`ly`, `cai`, etc.) for robust STT-style commands.
    - `services/ai-backend/tests/test_ai_backend.py`
      - Added regressions:
        - `test_generic_remove_with_quantity_decrements_last_item`
        - `test_generic_remove_with_number_words_decrements_last_item`
  - Validation:
    - Targeted asyncio pytest suite for add/remove quantity paths: 5 passed.
    - `python -m py_compile` for modified files passed.
  - Tradeoff:
    - `giam` now participates in remove intent when cart is non-empty; rare non-order context with this word may route into remove flow, but guarded by generic-remove checks to avoid accidental deletion.

- Enhance round 387 completed (auto-listen STT noise suppression for short accidental captures):
  - User pain point:
    - System kept reacting to tiny utterances/noise even after user stopped speaking; setting 300ms silence still produced accidental turns (`dat`, `em`).
  - Root cause:
    - `VOICE_ALWAYS_LISTEN` mode keeps microphone active by design; with short submit silence, one-token partial/final transcripts can be enqueued as real turns.
  - Fixes applied:
    - `apps/kiosk-ui/public/stitch_robot_3d_control_center.html`
      - Added `AUTO_STT_NOISE_SINGLE_TOKEN_BLOCKLIST` and `shouldIgnoreAutoTranscript(...)`.
      - `enqueueUserTurn(...)` now drops likely STT noise transcripts for non-manual sources:
        - single very short/filler tokens,
        - ultra-short 2-token filler patterns.
      - Keeps manual input untouched.
  - Validation:
    - `npm --prefix apps/kiosk-ui run build` passed.
  - Note:
    - 300ms now still works for responsiveness, but low-value accidental STT snippets are filtered before triggering backend turns.

- Debug/Enhance round 388 completed (STT finalize hang fix: speaks done but no reply):
  - User pain point:
    - After user finished speaking, kiosk kept listening/waiting and did not respond.
  - Root cause:
    - Backend STT finalize timer was effectively reset by continuous recorder chunks, causing missed/late finalize in some sessions.
    - `voiceBackendFinalizing` could become stale true if backend failed to return `final`, blocking future finalize attempts.
  - Fixes applied:
    - `apps/kiosk-ui/public/stitch_robot_3d_control_center.html`
      - Reworked `scheduleBackendFinalize()` into silence-aware checker:
        - no continuous reset storm,
        - finalize based on elapsed silence (`lastSpeechActivityAt`) rather than chunk cadence.
      - Added stuck-state recovery with `voiceBackendFinalizeIssuedAt`:
        - if finalize command is stale too long, auto-unblock and retry.
      - Updated force-finalize path with same stale recovery guard.
      - Reset finalize-issued timestamp on `final`, `onclose`, stop/start listening.
  - Validation:
    - `npm --prefix apps/kiosk-ui run build` passed.
  - Expected impact:
    - User finishes speaking -> system finalizes and replies reliably instead of waiting indefinitely.

- Debug round 389 completed (browser interim submit timer no longer starves on repeated same transcript):
  - User pain point:
    - Voice UI still stuck in `Dang nghe: ...` after user stopped speaking, no response triggered.
  - Root cause:
    - Browser SpeechRecognition emitted identical interim text repeatedly; `scheduleBrowserInterimSubmit(...)` reset timer every event, so `SUBMIT_SILENCE_MS` callback could be starved indefinitely.
  - Fixes applied:
    - `apps/kiosk-ui/public/stitch_robot_3d_control_center.html`
      - Added guard: if interim text is unchanged and submit timer already running, do not reset timer.
      - Improved timer state cleanup for pending interim timestamp bookkeeping.
  - Validation:
    - `npm --prefix apps/kiosk-ui run build` passed.
  - Expected impact:
    - For repeated identical interim outputs (e.g., `mot ca phe muoi`), submit timer now fires and enqueues turn reliably.

- Debug round 390 completed (browser STT still waiting after speech stop - robust silence-submit):
  - Symptom:
    - UI stayed at `Dang nghe: ...` and did not submit/respond after user finished speaking.
  - Root cause:
    - Browser interim submit path used debounce-like timeout reset behavior; small interim variations could keep postponing submit.
    - `lastSpeechActivityAt` was refreshed too eagerly on repeated interim content.
  - Fixes applied:
    - `apps/kiosk-ui/public/stitch_robot_3d_control_center.html`
      - Reworked `scheduleBrowserInterimSubmit(...)` into silence-aware checker (similar principle as backend finalize).
      - Timer now persists and re-checks elapsed silence instead of full reset cycles on interim updates.
      - Added forced-submit upper bound (`max(1800, submitSilenceMs * 8)`) to prevent indefinite wait.
      - Updated browser `onresult` to call `markSpeechActivity()` only when interim content changed meaningfully.
  - Validation:
    - `npm --prefix apps/kiosk-ui run build` passed.
  - Expected impact:
    - After user stops speaking, interim text should submit and trigger reply reliably (no endless waiting state).
- Debug round 391 completed (voice panel stuck on old interim text + next utterance dropped while robot busy):
  - Symptom:
    - Voice mini panel kept showing old `Dang nghe: ...` text.
    - User spoke next sentence while robot was replying, but system appeared to wait/treo and did not process follow-up reliably.
  - Evidence:
    - In `scheduleBrowserInterimSubmit`, branch `if (isConversationTurnBusy())` cleared `voiceBrowserPendingInterim` immediately, causing data loss.
    - In `enqueueUserTurn`, `browser-interim` source was hard-dropped while busy.
  - Root cause:
    - Interim transcript pipeline dropped valid utterances during busy window instead of deferring submit.
  - Fix applied:
    - `apps/kiosk-ui/public/stitch_robot_3d_control_center.html`
      - `scheduleBrowserInterimSubmit`: when busy, keep pending interim and reschedule check instead of clearing it.
      - Added status while waiting (`Robot dang phan hoi, da ghi nhan cau tiep theo...`) and status on submit (`Dang gui len backend...`) to avoid stale `Dang nghe: ...` feeling.
      - `enqueueUserTurn`: removed hard drop for `browser-interim` while busy; excluded `browser-interim` from rapid busy auto-drop filter.
  - Validation:
    - `npm --prefix apps/kiosk-ui run build` passed.
  - Remaining risk:
    - If user speaks many follow-ups during one long bot response, current design still keeps only latest pending interim (intended to avoid queue spam).
- Debug round 392 completed (voice status blinking + perceived no-listen/no-reply after busy-wait patch):
  - Symptom:
    - Voice status text flickered/chopped rapidly.
    - User felt robot was not listening/replying due unstable status updates.
  - Root cause:
    - Busy-wait loop in `scheduleBrowserInterimSubmit` updated status every retry tick (~100-220ms).
    - `setVoiceStatus` always rewrote DOM even when text/flag unchanged.
  - Fix applied:
    - `apps/kiosk-ui/public/stitch_robot_3d_control_center.html`
      - Added status dedup cache (`voiceLastStatusText`, `voiceLastStatusThinking`) in `setVoiceStatus` to skip identical updates.
      - In browser interim busy branch, show busy notice only once per submit cycle (`busyNoticeShown`) instead of every timer tick.
  - Validation:
    - `npm --prefix apps/kiosk-ui run build` passed.

    - Refresh page (F5) should start with clean chat history.

  - Symptom:
    - User pressed F5 but old chat still persisted.

- Enhance round 397 completed (stuck waiting due interim-drop race in browser STT):
  - Symptom:
    - Voice mini panel could stay at `Dang nghe: ...` and system seemed to wait forever without sending next turn.
  - Root cause:
    - `scheduleBrowserInterimSubmit('')` cleared pending interim immediately on empty interim events, causing transcript loss before enqueue.
    - Forced submit cap was too long (`submitSilenceMs * 8`), making perceived waiting worse in noisy/intermittent interim streams.
  - Fix applied:
    - `apps/kiosk-ui/public/stitch_robot_3d_control_center.html`
      - Empty interim now keeps pending interim (if present) instead of clearing it.
      - On pending-empty-interim state, shows status `Dang xu ly cau vua noi...`.
      - Reduced forced submit upper bound to `max(1200, submitSilenceMs * 2.5)` for faster handoff.
  - Validation:
    - `npm --prefix apps/kiosk-ui run build` passed.

- Enhance round 400 completed (stuck at "Dang gui len backend..." hardening):
  - Symptom:
    - Voice UI could appear stuck at "Dang gui len backend..." for too long.
    - Dev startup often reused existing ai-backend process, causing stale runtime behavior after code changes.
  - Fixes applied:
    - `scripts/dev-ai.ps1`
      - Disabled reuse-by-default for existing compatible ai-backend process.
      - New explicit opt-in: `-ReuseExisting` or env `AI_DEV_REUSE_EXISTING=1`.
      - Default behavior now restarts compatible listener to ensure latest code is loaded.
    - `apps/kiosk-ui/public/stitch_robot_3d_control_center.html`
      - Added frontend watchdog timeout for one turn (`MAX_BACKEND_TURN_WAIT_MS = 22000`).
      - If timeout is reached, abort turn and show clear recovery status (`Backend dang cham...`) instead of hanging forever.
  - Validation:
    - `npm --prefix apps/kiosk-ui run build` passed.
